name:L‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçu‚Äçj‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçt‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçd‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçd‚Äço‚Äçu

info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:I chose Huanglong Hotel again for my trip to Hangzhou during the Qingming Festival. It was the right decision. First of all, the surrounding environment is good, unlike the hotels near Fengqi Road subway station that I chose several times before. The transportation is convenient. There is a bus stop a few dozen meters from the south gate of the hotel. Bus 103 goes directly to Lingyin Temple, Meijiawu, Yunqi Bamboo Path, Jiuxi, and a few stops in the opposite direction to Wulin Gate. It is also very close to the Broken Bridge of West Lake and the cruise ship pier. It is very convenient. Less than 100 meters to the right of the South Gate is the A2 exit of Huanglong Cave on Line 3, and the A1 exit is across the road from the West Gate. Line 3 goes directly to Xixi Wetland South and Impression City, and we also went to Sam's Club for a stroll. The hotel breakfast is good, with a combination of Chinese and Western basics, as well as freshly baked Jinyun sesame cakes and freshly wrapped wontons. We lived in Building 5, which was a little far from the main south gate, but the West Gate was downstairs, and it was convenient to take the subway and taxi. The room was clean. The handheld shower was too heavy and too low. I could only use the fixed shower head on my head to wash my hair. It was the first time I saw such a heavy shower head. There were 8 small bottles of mineral water in the room, which was more generous than many hotels. The only drawback was that the price was a bit expensive during the Qingming Festival. The famous buffet restaurant's dinner was more than 400 per person, which was a bit disappointing. In general, if you have enough budget, I still recommend Huanglong Hotel.
